### <a name="apache-mahout-preinstalled-on-hdinsight-31"></a><span data-ttu-id="f7c35-1497">Apache Mahout preinstalado en HDInsight 3.1</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f7c35-1497">Apache Mahout preinstalled on HDInsight 3.1</span></span>

        mahout org.apache.mahout.classifier.df.tools.Describe -p /user/hdp/glass.data -f /user/hdp/glass.info -d I 9 N L

        mahout org.apache.mahout.classifier.df.BreimanExample -d /user/hdp/glass.data -ds /user/hdp/glass.info -i 10 -t 100

### <a name="dos--donts-between-cluster-versions"></a><span data-ttu-id="f7c35-1513">Qué se debe hacer y qué no se debe hacer entre versiones de clúster</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f7c35-1513">Dos & Don'ts between cluster versions</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="f7c35-1519">**Las tiendas de metadatos Oozie no se pueden compartir entre clústeres.**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f7c35-1519">**Oozie metastores cannot be shared across clusters.**</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="f7c35-1675">La versión 3.1 de HDInsight utiliza una distribución de Hadoop que se basa en hello [Hortonworks Data Platform 2.1.7][hdp-2-1-7].</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f7c35-1675">HDInsight version 3.1 uses a Hadoop distribution that is based on hello [Hortonworks Data Platform 2.1.7][hdp-2-1-7].</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f7c35-1676">Se trata de un clúster de Hadoop de hello predeterminado creado cuando se usa Hola portal de Azure después de 7/11/2014.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f7c35-1676">This is hello default Hadoop cluster created when using hello Azure portal after 11/7/2014.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="f7c35-1677">Clústeres de HDInsight 3.1 creados antes de 7/11/2014 se basaban en hello [Hortonworks Data Platform 2.1.1][hdp-2-1-1]</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="f7c35-1677">HDInsight 3.1 clusters created before 11/7/2014 were based on hello [Hortonworks Data Platform 2.1.1][hdp-2-1-1]</span></span>
